vnd.unilang:stripe.html>stripe</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:streak.html>streak</a>’, <a href = vnd.unilang:latvian.html>Latvian</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">ràibs</i> ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:spotted.html>spotted</a>’, <a href = vnd.unilang:russian.html>Russian</a> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рябой.html>рябо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjabój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:mottled.html>mottled</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fur.html>fur</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
